## Ejercicio 1: Limpieza y Transformación


```python
%%writefile mapper_filter.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

# 4, 6, 7

sys.stdin.readline()

for line in sys.stdin:
    words = line.strip().split(";")
    country_name = words[4]
    year = int(words[6])
    total_gdp = float(words[7])
    if year >= 2000 and total_gdp > 0:
        print(f"{country_name}\t{year}\t{total_gdp}")
```

    Overwriting mapper_filter.py



```python
%%writefile reducer_filter.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

for line in sys.stdin:
    print(line)
```

    Writing reducer_filter.py



```python
!cat countries_gdp_hist.csv | python3 mapper_filter.py
```


```python
!hdfs dfs -rm -r /patrones/salida/filter
!hadoop jar \
/usr/local/hadoop/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-3.4.0.jar \
-file mapper_filter.py \
-file reducer_filter.py \
-mapper mapper_filter.py \
-reducer reducer_filter.py \
-input /patrones/countries_gdp_hist.csv \
-output /patrones/salida/filter
```

## Ejercicio 2: Agregación por clave


```python
%%writefile mapper_hist_pib.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

sys.stdin.readline()

for line in sys.stdin:
    words = line.strip().split(";")
    region = words[1]
    total_gdp = words[7]
    
    print(f"{region}\t{total_gdp}")
```

    Overwriting mapper_hist_pib.py



```python
%%writefile reducer_hist_pib.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

current_region = None
current_gdp = 0

for line in sys.stdin:
    region, gdp = line.strip().split("\t")
    gdp = float(gdp)
    
    if current_region == region:
        current_gdp += gdp
    else:
        if current_region:
            print(f"{current_region}\t{current_gdp}")
            
        current_region = region
        current_gdp = gdp

print(f"{current_region}\t{current_gdp}")
```

    Overwriting reducer_hist_pib.py



```python
!cat countries_gdp_hist.csv | python3 mapper_hist_pib.py | sort | python3 reducer_hist_pib.py
```

## Ejercicio 3: Máximos por grupo (Filtering/Top-K)


```python
%%writefile mapper_gdp_var.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

sys.stdin.readline()

for line in sys.stdin:
    words = line.strip().split(";")
    country_name = words[4]
    year = words[6]
    gdp_var = words[-1]
    
    print(f"{country_name}\t{year},{gdp_var}")
```

    Overwriting mapper_gdp_var.py



```python
%%writefile reducer_gdp_var.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

current_country = None
current_gdp_var = 0
current_year = 0

for line in sys.stdin:
    country, num_data = line.strip().split("\t")
    year, gdp_var = num_data.split(",")
    gdp_var = abs(float(gdp_var))
    
    if current_country == country:
        if gdp_var >= current_gdp_var:     
            current_gdp_var = gdp_var
            current_year = year
    else:
        if current_country:
            print(f"{current_country}\t{current_year}, {current_gdp_var}")
            
        current_country = country
        current_gdp_var = gdp_var
        current_year = year

print(f"{current_country}\t{current_year}, {current_gdp_var}")
```

    Overwriting reducer_gdp_var.py



```python
!hdfs dfs -rm -r /patrones/salida/pib_var
!hadoop jar \
/usr/local/hadoop/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-3.4.0.jar \
-file mapper_gdp_var.py \
-file reducer_gdp_var.py \
-mapper mapper_gdp_var.py \
-reducer reducer_gdp_var.py \
-input /patrones/countries_gdp_hist.csv \
-output /patrones/salida/pib_var
```

## Ejercicio 4: Join (Reduce-Side Join)


```python
%%writefile mapper_country_code.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

sys.stdin.readline()

for line in sys.stdin:
    data = ""
    try:
        words = line.strip().split(";")
        data = f"{words[0]}\tB_{words[7]}"
    except IndexError:
        words = line.strip().split(",")
        data = f"{words[2]}\tA_{words[0]}"
    
    print(f"{data}")
```

    Overwriting mapper_country_code.py



```python
!cat countries_gdp_hist.csv | python3 mapper_country_code.py
```


```python
%%writefile reducer_country_code.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

current_code = None
current_country = None

for line in sys.stdin:
    code, data = line.strip().split("\t")
    
    if data[0] == "A":
        current_country = data[2:]
        current_code = code
    else:
        gdp = data[2:]
        if current_code == code:
            print(f"{current_code}\t{current_country}, {gdp}")

print(f"{current_code}\t{current_country}, {gdp}")
```

    Overwriting reducer_country_code.py



```python
!hdfs dfs -rm -r /patrones/salida/join
!hadoop jar \
/usr/local/hadoop/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-3.4.0.jar \
-files mapper_country_code.py,reducer_country_code.py \
-input /patrones/countries_gdp_hist.csv \
-input /patrones/codes.csv \
-mapper mapper_country_code.py \
-reducer reducer_country_code.py \
-output /patrones/salida/join
```

## Ejercicio 5: Distribución de Riqueza (Binning Pattern)


```python
%%writefile mapper_binning.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

sys.stdin.readline()

for line in sys.stdin:
    words = line.strip().split(";")
    gdp = float(words[7])

    category = None
    if gdp < 10000000:
        category = "Economía Pequeña"
    elif gdp < 1000000000:
        category = "Economía Mediana"
    else:
        category = "Economía Grande"
    
    print(f"{category}\t1")
```

    Overwriting mapper_binning.py



```python
%%writefile reducer_binning.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

current_category = None
current_count = 0

for line in sys.stdin:
    category, count = line.strip().split("\t")
    count = int(count)
    
    if current_category == category:
        current_count += count
    else:
        if current_category:
            print(f"{current_category}\t{current_count}")
            
        current_category = category
        current_count = 0

print(f"{current_category}\t{current_count}")
```

    Writing reducer_binning.py



```python
!hdfs dfs -rm -r /patrones/salida/binning
!hadoop jar \
/usr/local/hadoop/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-3.4.0.jar \
-file mapper_binning.py \
-file reducer_binning.py \
-mapper mapper_binning.py \
-reducer reducer_binning.py \
-input /patrones/countries_gdp_hist.csv \
-output /patrones/salida/binning
```

## Ejercicio 6: Índice invertido de países (Inverted Index Pattern)


```python
%%writefile mapper_inv_index.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

sys.stdin.readline()

for line in sys.stdin:
    words = line.strip().split(";")
    # 5 = income_group | 4 = country_name 
    print(f"{words[5]}\t{words[4]}")
```

    Writing mapper_inv_index.py



```python
%%writefile reducer_inv_index.py
#!/usr/bin/env python3

import sys

high_income = set()
low_income = set()

for line in sys.stdin:
    income_group, country_name = line.strip().split("\t")
    
    if income_group == "INGRESO ALTO":
        high_income.add(country_name)
    else:
        low_income.add(country_name)

print(f"INGRESO ALTO: {high_income}")
print()
print(f"INGRESO BAJO: {low_income}")
```

    Overwriting reducer_inv_index.py



```python
!cat countries_gdp_hist.csv | python3 mapper_inv_index.py | sort | python3 reducer_inv_index.py
```


```python
!hdfs dfs -rm -r /patrones/salida/inv_index
!hadoop jar \
/usr/local/hadoop/share/hadoop/tools/lib/hadoop-streaming-3.4.0.jar \
-file mapper_inv_index.py \
-file reducer_inv_index.py \
-mapper mapper_inv_index.py \
-reducer reducer_inv_index.py \
-input /patrones/countries_gdp_hist.csv \
-output /patrones/salida/inv_index
```
